        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="18302624" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="18302603" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1774" id="answer-18302624" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="18302624">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1774" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1774
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/18302624/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Since Android Studio uses
             <a href="http://tools.android.com/tech-docs/new-build-system/user-guide" rel="noreferrer">
              the new Gradle-based build system
             </a>
             , you should be
             <a href="http://tools.android.com/tech-docs/new-build-system/user-guide#TOC-Project-Structure" rel="noreferrer">
              putting
              <code>
               assets/
              </code>
              inside of the source sets
             </a>
             (e.g.,
             <code>
              src/main/assets/
             </code>
             ).
            </p>
            <p>
             In a typical Android Studio project, you will have an
             <code>
              app/
             </code>
             module, with a
             <code>
              main/
             </code>
             sourceset (
             <code>
              app/src/main/
             </code>
             off of the project root), and so your primary assets would go in
             <code>
              app/src/main/assets/
             </code>
             . However:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <p>
               If you need assets specific to a build type, such as
               <code>
                debug
               </code>
               versus
               <code>
                release
               </code>
               , you can create sourcesets for those roles (e.g,.
               <code>
                app/src/release/assets/
               </code>
               )
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Your product flavors can also have sourcesets with assets (e.g.,
               <code>
                app/src/googleplay/assets/
               </code>
               )
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Your instrumentation tests can have an
               <code>
                androidTest
               </code>
               sourceset with custom assets (e.g.,
               <code>
                app/src/androidTest/assets/
               </code>
               ), though be sure to ask the
               <code>
                InstrumentationRegistry
               </code>
               for
               <code>
                getContext()
               </code>
               , not
               <code>
                getTargetContext()
               </code>
               , to access those assets
              </p>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             Also, a quick reminder: assets are read-only at runtime. Use
             <a href="https://commonsware.com/blog/2014/04/07/storage-situation-internal-storage.html" rel="noreferrer">
              internal storage
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="https://commonsware.com/blog/2014/04/08/storage-situation-external-storage.html" rel="noreferrer">
              external storage
             </a>
             , or
             <a href="http://developer.android.com/guide/topics/providers/document-provider.html" rel="noreferrer">
              the Storage Access Framework
             </a>
             for read/write content.
            </p>
           </div>

              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @kalehv: "or do i need to assign the font explicitly by code to the control to see it?" -- oh, absolutely. You will need to call
                 <code>
                  setTypeface()
                 </code>
                 on all
                 <code>
                  TextView
                 </code>
                 widgets (and others that inherit from
                 <code>
                  TextView
                 </code>
                 ) that you want to use this particular font.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/115145/commonsware" title="951,527 reputation">
                  CommonsWare
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2013-08-18 19:10:34Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Aug 18, 2013 at 19:10
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/27673773/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              <em>
               Let Android Studio do it for you.
              </em>
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              In Android Studio (
              <em>
               1.0 &amp; above
              </em>
              ), right-click on the
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/zgcSy.png"/>
              folder and navigate to the
              <em>
               <code>
                Assets Folder
               </code>
              </em>
              .
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/nJuct.png"/>
            </p>
            <ol start="2">
             <li>
              On the next screen just click
              <em>
               <code>
                Finish
               </code>
              </em>
              .
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/q0t34.png"/>
            </p>
            <p>
             And voila! It will create the
             <em>
              <code>
               assets
              </code>
             </em>
             folder in the
             <em>
              <code>
               main
              </code>
             </em>
             target source set.
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/2o3SW.png"/>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="21254888">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="21254888" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="18302603" data-position-on-page="3" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="127" id="answer-21254888" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="21254888">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="127" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             127
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/21254888/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Looking inside the .iml file of your project you will see the following line:
            </p>
            <pre><code> &lt;option name="ASSETS_FOLDER_RELATIVE_PATH" value="/src/main/assets" /&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This means the "assets" folder is already declared for Gradle. You will need to create it under
             <code>
              src/main/
             </code>
             (I'm using Android Studio 0.4.2).
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2014-01-21T10:03:58" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="32407025">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Select the
             <code>
              app
             </code>
             folder and then:
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              <code>
               File
              </code>
             </strong>
             &gt;
             <strong>
              <code>
               New
              </code>
             </strong>
             &gt;
             <strong>
              <code>
               folder
              </code>
             </strong>
             &gt;
             <strong>
              <code>
               assets Folder
              </code>
             </strong>
             ,
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/Oxa83.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/Oxa83.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             the default location is inside
             <code>
              /main
             </code>
             folder
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/khAqo.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/khAqo.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/50907775/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             First of all the "Assets" folder will not be created automatically with the project. We have to create it.
            </p>
            <p>
             The location of Assets folder is:
             <strong>
              App &gt; src &gt; Assets
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             Please have a look of the simple image below.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/cGCyx.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/cGCyx.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Note:
             </strong>
             For creating assets folder just click on Project =&gt; Right click =&gt; Select New =&gt; Folder =&gt; Assets. It will create Assets folder.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

            <p>
             It's simple, follow these steps
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              File &gt; New &gt; Folder &gt; Assets Folder
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Note :
             </strong>
             App must be selected before creating folder.
            </p>

        <a name="27425778">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="27425778" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="18302603" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="31" id="answer-27425778" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="27425778">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="31" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             31
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/27425778/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In android studio you can specify where the source, res, assets folders are located.
for each module/app in the build.gradle file you can add something like:
            </p>
            <pre><code>android {
    compileSdkVersion 21
    buildToolsVersion "21.1.1"

    sourceSets {
        main {
            java.srcDirs = ['src']
            assets.srcDirs = ['assets']
            res.srcDirs = ['res']
            manifest.srcFile 'AndroidManifest.xml'
        }
    }
}
</code></pre>
           </div>

           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Click over main → new -&gt; directory → and type as name "assets"
            </p>
            <p>
             or... main -&gt; new -&gt; folder -&gt; assets folder (see image)

            <p>
             In Android Studio 4.1.1
            </p>
            <p>
             Right Click on your module (app for example) -&gt; New -&gt; Folder -&gt; Assets Folder
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/fj8zw.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/fj8zw.png"/>
             </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Two ways:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               Select app/main folder, Right click and select New =&gt; Folder =&gt; Asset Folder.
It will create 'assets' directory in main.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Select main folder, Right click and select New =&gt; Directory
Enter name as 'assets' = &gt; Ok.
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/nFVlK.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/nFVlK.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>

             It might not show on your side bar if the app is selected. Click the drop-down at the top that says android and select packages. you will see it then.

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             When upgrading to the release version of Android Studio, you may be automatically switched to the new Android project View (see
             <a href="https://developer.android.com/sdk/installing/studio-androidview.html" rel="noreferrer">
              here
             </a>
             for more info). If you swap back to either the Project or Packages view, you should see the standard folder hierarchy of a Gradle-based project. Then refer to
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/18302624/2911458">
              CommonsWare's answer
             </a>
             for the appropriate location.
            </p>

            <h2>
             Solution 2022
            </h2>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             <em>
              <strong>
               Project -&gt; app -&gt; src -&gt; main -&gt; RMB(right mouse button) -&gt; New -&gt; Directory:
              </strong>
             </em>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/EfO5C.png" rel="noreferrer">

             </a>

            <p>
             need configure parameter for gradle
             <br/>
             i hope is will work
            </p>
            <pre><code>// file: build.gradle  
sourceSets {
    main {
        assets.srcDirs = ['src/main/res/icon/', 'src/main/assets/']
    }
}
</code></pre>

           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In Android Studio, click on the
             <code>
              app
             </code>
             folder, then the
             <code>
              src
             </code>
             folder, and then the
             <code>
              main
             </code>
             folder. Inside the main folder you can add the assets folder.
            </p>

1)file-&gt;New-&gt;Folder
 there are multiple options like
      aidl folder
      assets folder
      jni folder
2) choose options assets folder
3) then there is option to change path of assets folder if you 
    want to change then check otherwise left that checkbox of cahnge folder location
4) click on finish 
</code></pre>

            <p>
             Either create a directory under /app/src/main or use studio File-&gt; New -&gt; Folder - &gt; Assets Folder.
            </p>

             In Android Studio right-click Folder in app-&gt;src-&gt;main then create new DIRECTORY name that
             <code>
              assets
